          <div class="t withAv">
           Get to level 17 and pick Paralyzing Palm as a perk. The rest is cake.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Also, Bannon from Rivet City will give you the schematics for a Deathclaw Gauntlet if you complete his unmarked quest in his favor (the one with Holmes). It has a crit multiplier of 5x, so if you have the Ninja perk (15% higher crit chance on unarmed and melee) (requires Melee weapons 80 and Sneak 80, plus level 20), and have 10 Luck, it will always score a critical hit while shredding completely through armor. Making one could be difficult, though. As Deathclaws are very dangerous.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Basically, unarmed focus is difficult at earlier levels, but once you get some of the high grade stuff and secure critical hits you can become really deadly. Leveling up in Sneak is also recommended, as sneak attacks secure critical hits and going full frontal into a pack of enemies is not adviced.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Also, you will face a lot of ranged enemies, making it near impossible to get away from a fight without taking damage, so level up Medicine skill too.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

          <div class="t withAv">
           To build upon your post, one can also get the schematics free from a picnic park on the south-western part of the map.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           There is a dead wastelander inside one of the trailers with the schematics nearby. The only problem is that there is a single deathclaw in the park, but it's not hard to kill it-- there are plenty of things you can jump on and make the AI confused. Best if you make it stuck near the car wrecks-- then all you need is to set one of them nuclear engines ablaze and it should make a chain reaction with the rest of the cars to kill the deathclaw.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Here is the location:
           <span class="spoiler">
            <span class="spoiler-icon">
             <!-- -->
            </span>
            <span class="spoiler-text">
             <a class="external_approved" href="http://img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120419213509/fallout/images/2/25/FSKT_Campground_loc.jpg" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120419213509/fallout/images/2/25/FSKT_Campground_loc.jpg">
              img2.wikia.nocookie.net/__cb20120419213509/fallout/images/2/25/FSKT_Campground_loc.jpg
             </a>
            </span>
           </span>
          </div>

          <div class="t withAv">
           I cant remember my build exactly, but I think my Str, End were fairly high. The ballistic fist requires high strength and you need to be able to take hits when approaching enemies, hence endurance. Endurance should give you points in survival so use that to your advantage. Cooking (Survival) and eating certain foods (steaks) from the camp fires is actually a pretty good method of health recovery. I put points in repair, survival, and unarmed. When starting out, you can find brass knuckles in Nevada Highway Patrol station on the way to the Mojave outpost. I can't remember the locations of unarmed weapons so you might have to look it. You can only buy or steal the ballistic fist off people, so I would recommend finding weapons you don't use, repair them, then sell them to make caps. Once you obtain the ballistic fist and decent armor , all you would have to worry about is keeping things in good condition. Weapons repair kits, which can be crafted with repair, will really help out and will also save you quite a bit of money.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           But that's just my build .  You could just take comradewinter's advice if you don't like mine.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           PS I was able to 1v1 deathclaws head-on with my build.
           <br/>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

           <div id="image_div123183549">
            <a href="http://new1.fjcdn.com/comments/The+storyline+is+different+the+variety+of+weapons+is+greater+_759c291632dcdc72692f9c42392d55ea.jpg" rel="lightbox" style="white-space:normal;">
             <img alt="The storyline is different, the variety of weapons is greater, the mechanics are different (armored enemies like hyperion units with a yellow health bar in comparison to armored enemies like skags who are still technically flesh)   
the characters are different, the world design is different.   
   
the same could be said for the pre-sequel.   
   
and you are wasting your time.   
if you dont like the game, dont buy it.   
you dont have to bitch about it on the internet because they didnt make a third installment." class="av_img" original="http://new1.fjcdn.com/thumbnails/comments/The+storyline+is+different+the+variety+of+weapons+is+greater+_759c291632dcdc72692f9c42392d55ea.jpg" src="http://new.fjcdn.com/site/funnyjunk/images/transparent_pixel.gif" style=" height:169px;"/>
            </a>
           </div>
           The storyline is different, the variety of weapons is greater, the mechanics are different (armored enemies like hyperion units with a yellow health bar in comparison to armored enemies like skags who are still technically flesh)
           <br/>
           the characters are different, the world design is different.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           the same could be said for the pre-sequel.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           and you are wasting your time.
           <br/>
           if you dont like the game, dont buy it.
           <br/>
           you dont have to bitch about it on the internet because they didnt make a third installment.
          </div>
         </div>

         <div class="t withAv">
          <div id="image_div123167574">
           <a href="http://new2.fjcdn.com/comments/I+m+taking+my+time+with+the+story+i+ve+just+_5ea20bc09367013dc051a4e9ef29ff39.jpg" rel="lightbox" style="white-space:normal;">
            <img alt="I'm taking my time with the story  I've just visited the awoken at lvl 20 . -I'm kinda enjoying the storyline, but maybe that's because I'm doing it fairly slow.    
-I enjoy the gameplay. Even though it just seems like shooting waves of enemies (which it just is, actually), I still enjoy it as I did with Borderlands, because at most enounters I still get this intense feeling of fighting through hordes of enemies without it going on for too long and become boring.    
-The gameplay feels good and the graphics are amazing.   
- I also like the fact that you can't acces certain areas because they are guarded by enemies with a too high level.    
-Color schemes (I am a sucker for every little thing you can customize).   
   
Now for the negative points:   
-The thing that is just non-existant in the game is some form of explanation. I get the grimoire cards give alot of lore, but I would've liked some real interaction with the Vanguard mentors or some other important characters. You get thrown into the story with the only motivation that if you don't do something, everything goes to 			*****		, and that's it.    
-Customization was exaggerated and overhyped. Every class has like two or three armor types per rarity color.    
-Patrol missions are very typical rpg fetch and kill quests. Also they give very little xp so I find it extremely irritating to grind my vanguard rank.   
-As the comic shows, loot is very rare and good loot is very, very rare. At least in PvE. I expected it to not be as lootbased as Borderlands but Destiny promoted it's customization and it's very hard to do that with so little (good) loot dropping.   
   
TL;DR   
   
It's a good game, though overhyped. I still give it a solid 7/10 for now, might get higher depending on the extra (free) daily/weekly/monthly updates they make." class="av_img" original="http://new2.fjcdn.com/thumbnails/comments/I+m+taking+my+time+with+the+story+i+ve+just+_5ea20bc09367013dc051a4e9ef29ff39.jpg" src="http://new.fjcdn.com/site/funnyjunk/images/transparent_pixel.gif" style=" height:169px;"/>
           </a>
          </div>
          I'm taking my time with the story
          <span class="spoiler">
           <span class="spoiler-icon">
            <!-- -->
           </span>
           <span class="spoiler-text">
            I've just visited the awoken at lvl 20
           </span>
          </span>
          . -I'm kinda enjoying the storyline, but maybe that's because I'm doing it fairly slow.
          <br/>
          -I enjoy the gameplay. Even though it just seems like shooting waves of enemies (which it just is, actually), I still enjoy it as I did with Borderlands, because at most enounters I still get this intense feeling of fighting through hordes of enemies without it going on for too long and become boring.
          <br/>
          -The gameplay feels good and the graphics are amazing.
          <br/>
          - I also like the fact that you can't acces certain areas because they are guarded by enemies with a too high level.
          <br/>
          -Color schemes (I am a sucker for every little thing you can customize).
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Now for the negative points:
          <br/>
          -The thing that is just non-existant in the game is some form of explanation. I get the grimoire cards give alot of lore, but I would've liked some real interaction with the Vanguard mentors or some other important characters. You get thrown into the story with the only motivation that if you don't do something, everything goes to
          <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
           *****
          </a>
          , and that's it.
          <br/>
          -Customization was exaggerated and overhyped. Every class has like two or three armor types per rarity color.
          <br/>
          -Patrol missions are very typical rpg fetch and kill quests. Also they give very little xp so I find it extremely irritating to grind my vanguard rank.
          <br/>
          -As the comic shows, loot is very rare and good loot is very, very rare. At least in PvE. I expected it to not be as lootbased as Borderlands but Destiny promoted it's customization and it's very hard to do that with so little (good) loot dropping.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          TL;DR
          <br/>
          <br/>
          It's a good game, though overhyped. I still give it a solid 7/10 for now, might get higher depending on the extra (free) daily/weekly/monthly updates they make.
         </div>
        </div>

          <div class="t withAv">
           It seems to me that you get better equipment in PVP, though you have to play usually (it seems) around three matches before you get anything. And the loot in PVP is randomized in kind of a
           <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
            ******
           </a>
           way. You can go 20 and 0 in a match, carry your team to victory, and get
           <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
            *******
           </a>
           nothing. Meanshile, some scrub who got one kill and died thirteen times gets an armor shader and a blue engram. Which is good if you're the scrub, but you should have a higher chance to get
           <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
            ****
           </a>
           if you do better.

           But I had a bunch of level 18-19 stuff from PVE and then got a bunch of 16-17 stuff in PVP that was just better in every single way than the stuff I got in PVE.
           <br/>

          <div class="t withAv">
           It's like Borderlands. It's free roam with certain locations where enemies spawn. A subtle difference is that in Borderlands, you have to load everytime you enter a building of sorts, while in destiny you load e.g. the moon, you can explore the whole map without loading screens, even when you enter buildings. Another difference is that in BL, the singleplayer was really a single player. In destiny, you are always online and you often run into other players, even if they aren't in your party. However, this is only in the wide open spaces. When you enter a small indoor area, other players dissapear, except when they are in your party.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           It's nothing like fallout, at leat imo. Maybe the feeling is the same when you walk through the ruins in old russia and venus, that feeling of something beautifull and vibrant that is now destroyed. But other than that the gamepay doesn't resemble fallout.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Hope this helped!
          </div>
         </div>

          <div class="t withAv">
           To gain a lot of rep you have to do bounties. If your gonna do patrols try looking for assassination ones. 2 of those will give enough rep to equal 1 bounty. Once you reach a certain level white drops become green and greens are replaced with blue. So you'll no longer get common stuff. I'd recommend sticking with the faction that suites your needs. Look around and see what they all have to offer.
          </div>

           Dont be too hasty, honestly the main thing i find fun about it is the animations you can do anywhere. There is NO story, i was chugging through it waiting for it to get good an interesting then the abysmal end cutscene happened suddenly. Nothing is explained, just typical "This is only the beginning crap". And the multiplayer is a pathetic joke, imagine running around with one hit kill OP god powers and OP god mode invincibility perks (With your main super power you can upgrade it so you're invincible whilst doing it, shot someone with a rocket earlier in the chest and they walked).

          <div class="t withAv">
           I gotta agree with you. I got the game because I was bored and had some small interest in the game. It got really over-hyped. The game is a 6 /10 at best. The graphics and gameplay are good, but the story is non-existent. Playing with friends does make the game better, but the entire thing is just a gear grind in the end. You go through the highest level missions and pray to find gear better than what you have but it's statistically improbable. The competitive multiplayer also entails the majority of players just running around with shotguns and then using their powers to continuously do whatever the
           <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
            ****
           </a>
           they want. The weapons system needs a major rebalance because there's no reason that my semi-auto rifle shouldn't fire as fast as I can pull the trigger and still do less than an automatic weapon. The game is better with friends, but hopefully they can get their
           <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
            ****
           </a>
           together with any and all DLC they release.

         <div class="t withAv">
          My biggest gripe about Destiny is the lack of story. Im more of a campaign person because I really like the stories better then getting into a pissing contest with some random stranger. Being Bungie, I expected a somewhat grabbing story. I knew we would never get the same level as they did with halo because this is mainly a multiplayer game, But I still wanted more. The only hint of story involves the robot chick and she's only there for maybe 2 minutes. Nothing I do in the game feels like it matters and the only person who even talks is the Ghost telling me obvious crap like more enemies are coming in or how Ill have to fight through 3 waves of enemies because he needs time to open a door.

         <div class="t withAv">
          <div id="image_div123182997">
           <img alt="Destiny is like Titanfall. 			*******		 of hype. 			*******		 of people who bought it day one. Everybody will forget about it after a month and bitterly regret those $60/60/50. Another example? The so called &quot;GTA V killer&quot; as it was called during development. Doesn't ring any bell? I don't blame you. I'm talking about Watch Dogs.   
   
What's even funnier is that Bungie said that Destiny has the potential to be on the shelves of people, sitting right next to the great franchises. Those guys made Halo for 			******		 sake, and they shat out a game overly repetitive with no story whatsoever. And don't even get me started on the AI. They keep hitting invisible walls and peacefully go back to their positions until you come closer again. I mean 			****		, the Covenants' AI's in Halo were so good. They were responsive, they always tried to flank you, the Elites were actually issuing orders, they were a force to be reckoned with. So when you hear that Bungie made another FPS, it's only natural to expect great AI programming and an epic story with a few ridiculously charismatic and badass characters.   
   
The environments are gorgeous, no doubts about that. They kept their promise on that. But it all feels... Empty. The environments are barely worth exploring and for a Borderlands-like (let's be honest here guys, Destiny is just Bungie's take on Borderlands) that's unforgivable.   
   
The bosses? They are hard to kill, but not hard as in challenging. They just made a big enemy with an overkill amount of HP. You might as well do a Lord of the Ring marathon and the 			******		 will still have a quarter of his life left.   
   
And that's just for the &quot;campaign&quot;. The PvP is a complete joke.   
   
I'm sorry but just like all the other recent AAA titles, it feels highly unfinished and is NOT worth its full retail price. Seriously guys, you want a better Destiny? Go play Warframe. It's on Steam, it's free and it can run on a goddamn potato battery." class="av_img" original="http://new1.fjcdn.com/thumbnails/comments/Destiny+is+like+titanfall+of+hype+of+people+_47d86de52bb92ee874bc3fb4e57096ff.gif" src="http://new.fjcdn.com/site/funnyjunk/images/transparent_pixel.gif" style=" height:168px;"/>
          </div>
          Destiny is like Titanfall.
          <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
           *******
          </a>
          of hype.
          <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
           *******
          </a>
          of people who bought it day one. Everybody will forget about it after a month and bitterly regret those $60/60/50. Another example? The so called "GTA V killer" as it was called during development. Doesn't ring any bell? I don't blame you. I'm talking about Watch Dogs.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          What's even funnier is that Bungie said that Destiny has the potential to be on the shelves of people, sitting right next to the great franchises. Those guys made Halo for
          <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
           ******
          </a>
          sake, and they shat out a game overly repetitive with no story whatsoever. And don't even get me started on the AI. They keep hitting invisible walls and peacefully go back to their positions until you come closer again. I mean
          <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
           ****
          </a>
          , the Covenants' AI's in Halo were so good. They were responsive, they always tried to flank you, the Elites were actually issuing orders, they were a force to be reckoned with. So when you hear that Bungie made another FPS, it's only natural to expect great AI programming and an epic story with a few ridiculously charismatic and badass characters.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The environments are gorgeous, no doubts about that. They kept their promise on that. But it all feels... Empty. The environments are barely worth exploring and for a Borderlands-like (let's be honest here guys, Destiny is just Bungie's take on Borderlands) that's unforgivable.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          The bosses? They are hard to kill, but not hard as in
          <em>
           challenging
          </em>
          . They just made a big enemy with an overkill amount of HP. You might as well do a Lord of the Ring marathon and the
          <a class="forUnlogged" href="#" onclick="users.showLoginForm(window.location);return false;" style="display:inline" title="Register Or Login to View Text">
           ******
          </a>
          will still have a quarter of his life left.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          And that's just for the "campaign". The PvP is a complete joke.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          I'm sorry but just like all the other recent AAA titles, it feels highly unfinished and is NOT worth its full retail price. Seriously guys, you want a better Destiny? Go play Warframe. It's on Steam, it's free and it can run on a goddamn potato battery.
         </div>

             <img alt="I'm really, really glad someone wrote that for me.

I've had my fun with Watch Dogs, since I didn't have ps3 and didn't want to take the x360 out of the basement (it's there somewhere I don't know), WD was the only open world city type of a game for PC at that moment. Plus some pretty cool features like being a vigilante, being able to make some choices and I actually loved the graphics with 'The Worst' mod and the music was fine, etc.    
   
Basically that one week of playing Watch Dogs was pretty good. I don't think I'll install it any soon but I kinda got it for little less than 20 EUR so I can't complain.    
   
Destiny on the other hand is enforced to be priced at around 60 EUR, has little to no interaction between players and plays just like Halo with reskinned enemies + some ripoffs from Borderlands.            is going on?
